FINANCE AGENDA

SEPTEMBER

8, 2005

The Finance Agenda Poll, Bids Report (Section I), and Highway Bills dated July 25, 2005 were
previously approved by poll on July 29, 2005. In accordance with Rule 4-2(c), the vote on the poll
taken 7/29/05 is as follows: 12 Yeas; and 5 Divided (Chairman Daley, Commissioners Hansen,
Moreno, Peraica and Silvestri). Chairman Daley voted present on Communication Number 272140.
With respect to Communication Number 272237, Chairman Daley voted present on the claims
regarding Thorek Hospital, Mercy Hospital, and Mercy Anesthesiologist Group. With respect to the
Highway Bills, Chairman Daley voted present on Section: 04-IFGFM-08-GM regarding G.F.
Structures Corporation. Commissioner Hansen voted present on Communication Numbers 272161
and 272162. With respect to the Bids Report, Commissioner Hansen voted no on Contract Nos. 0573-66 Rebid , 05-84-153, and 05-73-172. Commissioner Moreno voted present on Communication
Numbers 272057, 272152, 272225, and 272199. Commissioner Peraica voted no on Communication
With respect the Bids Report,
Numbers 272229, 272154, 272160, 272224, and 272228.
Commissioner Peraica voted no on Contract No. 05-73-172. Commissioner Silvestri voted no on
Communication Number 272225.
The Finance Agenda Poll, Bids Reports (Sections I, IA, IB and II), and Highway Bills dated August 15,
2005 were previously approved by poll on August 19, 2005. In accordance with Rule 4-2(c), the vote
on the poll taken 8/19/05 is as follows: 9 Yeas; and 8 Divided (Chairman Daley, Commissioners
Gorman, Hansen, Moreno, Peraica, Quigley, Silvestri and Suffredin). Chairman Daley voted present
on Communication Numbers 272365 and 272377. With respect to the Highway Bills, Chairman Daley
voted present on Section: 98-A5019-03-EG regarding McDonough Associates, Inc. Commissioner
Gorman voted no on Communication Number 272500. Commissioner Hansen voted present on
Communication Numbers 272432, 272433 and 272434.
With respect to the Bids Reports,
Commissioner Hansen voted no on Contract Nos. 05-54-328, 05-15-035H and 05-15-285H.
Commissioner Moreno voted present on Communication Numbers 272281 , 272379, 272381 and
272382. With respect to the Bids Reports, Commissioner Moreno voted present on Contract No. 0515-035H. Commissioner Peraica voted no on Communication Numbers 272500, 272406 and 272435.
With respect to the Bids Reports, Commissioner Peraica voted no on Contract Nos. 05-54-387, 05-72422, 05-54-328 and 05-82-34. Commissioner Quigley voted no on Communication Number 272281.
With respect to the Bids Reports, Commissioner Silvestri voted present on Contract No. 04-82-830
Rebid. Commissioner Suffredin voted no on Communication Numbers 272281 and 272500. With
respect to the Bids Reports, Commissioner Suffredin voted no on Contract Nos. 04-84-847, 04-85-878
Rebid, 05-82-332 Rebid, 05-54-387 and 05-54-362.

I NDUSTRIAL COMMISSION CLAIMS
THE FOLLOWING INDUSTRIAL COMMISSION CLAIMS SUBMITTED BY RICHARD A . DEVINE, STATE'S
ATTORNEY, RECOMMENDING PAYMENT TO THE FOLLOWING CLAIMANTS FOR INJURIES SUSTAINED IN THE
COURSE OF THEIR EMPLOYMENT, HAVE BEEN APPROVED AND RECOMMENDED FOR PAYMENT BY THE
INDUSTRIAL CLAIMS SUBCOMMITTEE :

272161

KASSIM DEEB, in the course of his employment as a Police Officer for the Sheriff's
Police Department sustained accidental injuries on September 10, 2001 . The
Petitioner's squad car was struck by another motor vehicle , and as a result he injured
his lower back (bulging disc at C5-C6). The County paid a total of $6,777.57 in
temporary total disability and $17, 344.41 in medical expenses. The County is entitled
to recover 75% of that amount, which is $18,091.47. The County has agreed to waive
$18,091.47 of its lien in exchange for a $1 .00 lump sum settlement contract. The
Industrial Commission approved the $1 .00 settlement contract on June 22, 2005.
State's Attorney, Richard A. Devine, is submitting Industrial Commission Lump Sum
Petition and Order No. 01-WC-64734 in the amount of $1.00 and recommends its
payment. (Finance Subcommittee June 8, 2005). Attorney: Timothy E. Takash, Law
Firm of Gregorio & Associates .
*This item was previously approved by poll on 7/29/2005

272162

DENITA WYNNE, in the course of her employment as a Juvenile Detention Counselor
for the Juvenile Temporary Detention Center sustained accidental injuries on June 21 ,
1999 and May 16, 2001. The June 21 , 1999 accident occurred when the Petitioner
slipped on spilled food , and as a result she injured her left knee (left knee strain). The
May 16, 2001 accident occurred when the Petitioner had an altercation with residents,
and as a result she injured her right arm (epicondylitis of the right elbow). On May 25,
2005, the Arbitrator awarded the Petitioner $16,429.76. State's Attorney, Richard A
Devine, is submitting Industrial Commission Decision of Arbitrator, Award Nos. 02WC-31871 and 03-WC-5717 in the amount of $16,429.76 and recommends its
payment. (Finance Subcommittee July 11, 2005). Attorney: John Lusak, Law Firm of
Lusak & Cobb.
* This item was previously approved by poll on 7/29/2005

272687

DOLLY ANTHONY, in the course of her employment as a Court Clerk for the Clerk of
the Circuit Court sustained accidental injuries on August 15, 2002. The Petitioner was
injured while entering an elevator when the door malfunctioned and slammed shut,
and as a result she injured her left shoulder and left knee (left shoulder sprain and
tendonitis; left knee sprain and tendonitis). State's Attorney, Richard A. Devine, is
submitting Industrial Commission Lump Sum Petition and Order No. 02-WC-59638 in
the amount of $5,000.00 and recommends its payment. (Finance Subcommittee July
11 , 2005). Attorney: Daniel M. Anders, Law Firm of Wiedner & McAuliffe, Ltd.

272688

SHARON D. BAHENA, in the course of her employment as a Deputy Sheriff for the
Sheriff's Office sustained accidental injuries on January 20, 2000. The Petitioner was
on an elevator that dropped, and as a result she injured her head, foot and ankle
(concussion, lis franc fractures to her foot and ankle developed reflex sympathetic
dystrophy syndrome). The County paid a total of $124,109.58 in temporary total
disability and $63, 399.42 in medical expenses. The County is entitled to recover 75%
of that amount, which is $140,631.75. The County has agreed to waive $90,631.75 of
its lien in exchange for a $1 .00 lump sum settlement contract to end the County's
ongoing liability. The Industrial Commission approved the $1.00 settlement contract
on July 28, 2005. State's Attorney, Richard A. Devine, is submitting Industrial
Commission Lump Sum Petition and Order No. 01 -WC-20657 in the amount of $1.00
and recommends its payment. (Finance Subcommittee July 11 , 2005). Attorney:
Charles G. Haskins, Law Firm of Cullen, Haskins, Nicholson & Menchetti.

 FINANCE AGENDA
SEPTEMBER 8, 2005
PAGE 54

272689

KEVIN BARRETT, in the course of his employment as a Clinical Nurse for the
Ambulatory and Community Health Network of Cook County sustained accidental
injuries on May 31, 2002. The Petitioner opened a file cabinet, which tipped and fell ,
and as a result he injured his right leg (right ankle sprain, right knee patellofemoral
syndrome). State's Attorney, Richard A. Devine, is submitting Industrial Commission
Lump Sum Petition and Order No. 02-WC-35193 in the amount of $8,158.67 and
recommends its payment. (Finance Subcommittee June 8, 2005). Attorney: Wayne
L. Newman, Law Firm of Horwitz, Horwitz and Associates, Ltd.

272690

MATTHEW MANION, in the course of his employment as a Deputy Sheriff for the
Sheriff's Court Services Division sustained accidental injuries on April 5, 2004. The

272236

THE EMPLOYEES' INJURY COMPENSATION COMMITTEE, submitting invoices
totaling $20,473.15, for payment of medical bills for Workers' Compensation cases
incurred by Forest Preserve District employees injured on duty. Individual checks will
be issued by the Comptroller in accordance with the attached report prepared by the
Department of Risk Management, Workers' Compensation Unit. Reimbursement by
the Forest Preserve District financial department will be made to the County
Comptroller on a monthly basis. This request covers bills received and processed
from June 22 through July 25, 2005.
